lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">《中国大陆良心犯数据库》不但收录了目前在押的这个良心犯、政治犯，已经获释、死亡的良心犯、政治犯也在此数据库中可以查询到。《中国大陆良心犯数据库》收集工作整理自<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月开始，截至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">01</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日共 收录良心犯资料共<span lang="EN-US">3611</span>人。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本报告主要关注的对象是所有在押的政治犯、良心犯——这里包括已被判刑的和羁押未判的——所有我们能够收集到确切信息的政治犯、良心犯。本报告竭力就包括汉、藏、维、哈萨克、回、蒙古、朝鲜、满等中国大陆多族裔政治犯、良心犯在内的信息进行收集、撰写和编辑，力求全面真实反映当前中国大陆政治犯、良心犯的恶劣的生存境遇。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">本报告为了便于人们查询检索，完全以良心犯、政治犯的姓名拼音顺序制作了完整的在押人员名录。同时，本报告仍对所有良心犯、政治犯的刑期进行了统计，羁押未判的也全部列于最后。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">本报告名单人员一旦取保候审、保外就医、无罪释放、回家监视居住、缓刑或刑满释放，都将从报告正式在押名单中移除，但其简历将显示于本期报告中。 <span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">本报告每月不辍，期期更新，其中凝聚了许多义工、信息员和编辑长期以来默默无闻的辛劳和奉献。</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">9</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年来，本网一共收集、整理、编辑过的有较为翔实资料的人员名单及其简历超过<span lang="EN-US">3000</span>多个<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">这个数字里内涵着本网所有工作人员在高度风险下的巨大付出。</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">本报告之所以能够按时定期发布，并且信息越来越翔实，这也得到了大陆许多人权捍卫者的积极反馈和支持。本网对所有提供信息的朋友，在此一并予以感谢。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">九年多如一日，本网持续不断地对中国大陆政治犯、良心犯境况进行总结和报告，是为了抗议谴责中共当局以超期羁押、拖延审判、虐待折磨、殴打等各种方式对良心犯政治犯施加酷刑，而在中共狱中被酷刑虐待折磨是被关押者要经常面对的严酷现实。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">本网坚信，外界坚持不懈的关注，将会给狱中受难者以精神和实质的援助！本报告一直对中共当局使用各种酷刑手段迫害折磨政治犯、良心犯的行径予以的系统揭露，业已引起了海内外各个方面的强烈反响。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本网一直在及时更新、统计最新讯息，每月末发布这月度报告，谨以此表达我们对所有失去自由的政治犯、良心犯的关注和牵挂。并以此，告诉全世界不要忘记这些为自由、民主、人权而承担苦难的人们。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本网认为，本报告的定期更新和发布，可以直接反映出大陆当下的人权概况——因为一个国家的政治犯、良心犯的境况是这个国家最重要的人权指标之一。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本网</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">以此</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">揭示中国大陆当下恶劣的人权概况与良心犯、政治犯的悲惨处境，力求唤起国际社会对中国在押政治犯、良心犯的记忆，并予以持续不断的关注和呼吁，直至他们获得自由。</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本网认为，定期将良心犯、政治犯的姓名和境况公诸于世，是我们能给予这些受难者以实际而有效支持的一种方式。我们深知，没有比被人们的遗忘更令这些良心犯、政治犯感到绝望和痛苦的事情。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">因此，我们必须肩负起这项工作，乃至是使命。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">九年多的风风雨雨已经过去，未来的道路上还会有千难万险，但是有你们的支持，我们仍将一如既往勇往直前！<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">最后，本报告虽经本网信息中心认真核查，并得到中国大陆许多人权捍卫者协助，但仍因条件所限，无法做到适时、准确统计全部在押政治犯、良心犯信息，报告所反映的只是冰山之一角，仍然是一份不完全的报告，这需要我们的继续努力！<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">如发现纰漏之处和补充信息，敬请指正，并尽可能知会本网。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoListParagraph" style="mso-list: l8 level1 lfo25; text-indent: -36.0pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: Roman&quot;;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></span></b><!--[endif]--><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本期报告概述：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">《维权网：中国大陆在押政治犯、良心犯月度报告》月月更新，是一份关于中国在押政治犯、良心犯的动态报告。此为第<span lang="EN-US">112</span>期。至此，本报告月月发布历时已整整九年多。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本期报告全文共计</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">五万六千字</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">。本期报告对上期报告的所有政治犯、良心犯名单进行了一次全面的逐一核查。获悉上期名单中</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">30</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">人已被</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">刑满释放或取保获释。并获悉有被羁押的<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人被判刑，<span lang="EN-US">12</span>人狱中有新动态，</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">同时，本期新增了我们又搜集的被刑事拘留<span lang="EN-US">/</span>被精神病<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人以及被判刑的<span lang="EN-US">57</span>人，合计<span lang="EN-US">61</span>人的名单及简介。目前，被本期报告录入姓名发布的在押良心犯、政治犯共</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">1682</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">人。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">为便于人们查询，《维权网：中国大陆在押政治犯、良心犯名单索引》为本报告名单的唯一索引。索引是以姓名拼音顺序排列（<span lang="EN-US">ABCDEFG....WXYZ</span>）。同时，本报告对所有良心犯、政治犯的刑期进行了统计，羁押未判的也全部列于最后。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><a name="_Hlk183794101"></a><a name="_Hlk175883967"></a><a name="_Hlk189095637"></a><a name="_Hlk162449568"></a><a name="_Hlk175727158"></a><a name="_Hlk181147271"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175727158;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk189095637;"><span _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk189095637;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183794101;"><span &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘艳涛、聂梅凤、陕富荣、石香云、孙丽华、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: lang="EN-US">10</span>日石家庄市深泽县十多名法轮功学员半夜被突然抓捕，其中杜国防等八人一直被关押在石家庄市第二看守所和晋州市看守所，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日被构陷到晋州市法院，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日在晋州市法院被开庭，据<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日获悉，把人均已被判刑。杜国防被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span></span></span></span></span><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/6/11/461862.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk189095637;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183794101;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">四川甘孜藏区炉霍县人，藏族人权捍卫者。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，在西藏康区炉霍县境内发生大规模和平示威活动后，中共军警釆取武力镇压，导致云丹为首的多名藏人被开枪打死或打伤，上百人遭捕。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日中共当局对<span lang="EN-US">16</span>名遭捕的藏人进行判决，其中一名藏人被判终身监禁，另有多人遭<span lang="EN-US">1</span>至<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年不等的有期徒刑。这<span lang="EN-US">16</span>名被判藏人中，已确切得知的有<span lang="EN-US">10</span>名藏人具体情况，其中：根托，现年<span lang="EN-US">20</span>多岁，被判<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年徒刑，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">广州市海珠区法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1968</span>年出生，大专毕业，吉林省德惠市人。她于<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年开始修炼法轮功，十几年来屡遭中共迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年，胡吉秀被海珠区昌岗派出所警察抓捕，同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，她被海珠区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，缓刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月四日，她被越秀区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月才从广东省女子监狱回家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日和<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，胡吉秀在海珠区工业大道沿线和越秀区张贴真相粘贴，遭监控拍摄。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，她被海珠区公安分局警察抓捕，并被抄家。<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月九日被海珠区检察院批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，被构陷到海珠区检察院。七、<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月份，被构陷到海珠区法院。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，胡吉秀被海珠区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，被罚金一万元。她认为判决，向广州市中级法院提起上诉。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，广州市中级法院维持原判。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span></span></span></span></span><a _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk189095637;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183794101;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">石家庄市深泽县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1949</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月出生，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">74</span>岁，河北省深泽县东北留村。因为修炼法轮功，自<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">720</span>后被中共当局多次关押迫害，遭受酷刑。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日石家庄市深泽县十多名法轮功学员半夜被突然抓捕，其中何红彦、刘小妙、杜国防等八人一直被关押在石家庄市第二看守所和晋州市看守所，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日被构陷到晋州市法院，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日在晋州市法院被开庭，据<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日获悉，把人均已被判刑。刘小妙被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span></span></span></span></span><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/6/11/461862.html"><span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。后刘艳涛被送唐山市冀东监狱关押。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk189095637;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183794101;"><span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">湖北省襄阳市老河口市法轮功学员，男，<span lang="EN-US">1965</span>年生，家住襄阳市老河口市，原湖北省江山机械厂护卫队员。陕富荣因坚持信仰法轮功，被中共迫害的家破人亡。他曾多次被抓捕，被囚在看守所、洗脑班、劳教所、监狱近十年，遭受非人折磨，几近丧命。陕富荣<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日在谷城县传播法轮功真相时被抓捕、关押在谷城县看守所，之后信息全无。现得知，陕富荣已被秘密判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，被关押在湖北省荆门市沙洋县范家台监狱，而且已经被迫害致双目失明。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span></span></span></span></span><a mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1968</span>年生，女。唐增叶于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日凌晨四点被大庆市公安局东安分局警察入室抓捕、抄家抢劫，关押在大庆第二看守所。唐增叶绝食反迫害，身体非常虚弱，被强行灌浓盐水，几次到医院检查身体，就是不放人。后来她不绝食了，但吃东西就吐。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日唐增叶被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span></span></span></span></span><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/1/13/454832.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183794101;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1938</span>年生，河北遵化市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，遵化多个村镇的数十名法轮功学员几乎同时在凌晨<span lang="EN-US">3</span>点多遭到警察的入室抓捕、抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，许昌魏都区法院法官判处王永胜有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，并罚金人民币三千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span></span></span></span></span><a lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，中共开始疯狂迫害法轮功后，徐润叶曾在内蒙古被抓捕，被关押在看守所迫害很长时间。后徐润叶再被抓捕、关押，曾被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半，在宁夏女子监狱遭受迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，徐润叶结束三年半冤狱，从宁夏女子监狱回家。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日因张贴法轮功真相传单，被银川市公安局金凤区分局长城中路派出所警察抓捕、构陷，近日被银川市西夏区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。目前被关押在银川市看守所<span lang="EN-US">.</span>刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">吉林省德惠市法轮功学员，男，德惠市大房身镇人。原是德惠市杨树粮库粮政管理员，中共发动迫害法轮功前曾担任法轮功义务辅导员。中共迫害法轮功后，赵金敏多次被绑架，遭<span lang="EN-US">3</span>次劳教。他的妻子马景环也是法轮功学员，至少和他一起遭两次绑架迫害、拘留，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年冬马景环含冤去世。赵金敏<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日遭德惠市公安局警察抓捕、抄家，关押在看守所构陷。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月获悉，赵金敏遭德惠市政法委、<span lang="EN-US">610</span>操控检察院起诉、法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span></span></span></span></span><a mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">四川省南充市法轮功学员，女。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日早，南充市高坪区公安分局政保大队警察闯入法轮功学员陈代友、邓国君夫妇的家非法抄家，抄走了法轮功书籍及电脑、打印机、影像制品等私人物品。警察把陈代友、邓国君夫妇绑架到高坪公安分局分别作笔录，直到晚上十一点多才让他们取保候审回家。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，高坪区警察又通知邓国君去高坪公安政保大队，问她是否把他们警察做恶的事曝光到了明慧网，说她与境外有联系。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，高坪区检察院检察官把构陷邓国君的案子移送到高坪区法院。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月邓国君女士被高坪区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日被抓捕关进看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。</span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk189095637;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183794101;"><b _Hlk189095637;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183794101;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日早上，罗美林被九江市柴桑区警方抓捕，随即遭刑事拘留、批捕、起诉。后罗美林被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，目前，她被关押在九江市看守所，她将被留在看守所坐牢役，直到她的刑期结束。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">湖南省临澧县法轮功学员，女，生于一九六二年十二月，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">62</span>岁，家住临澧县安福镇，于一九九八年八月开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，临澧县公安局、安福镇派出所、望城乡派出所出动大量警力，到法轮功学员家进行抓捕，其中有胡月英，随即被送到常德市看守所关押。后遭批捕、起诉，最终被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月中旬胡月英被转监到湖南省长沙女子监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<span _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk189095637;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183794101;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk189095637;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183794101;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、许艳：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk189095637;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183794101;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1982</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日出生，天津市人，北京市石景山区八角北路<span lang="EN-US">24</span>楼租住居民，人权律师余文生之妻，基督徒，推特账号<span lang="EN-US">l@xuyan709</span>，<span lang="EN-US"> 709</span>维权系列案家属之一，人权捍卫者，中国在押政治犯。自从与人权律师余文生结婚以后，夫妻感情甚笃，且一直支持丈夫对自由民主及人权理念的追求；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年，曾为丈夫因涉嫌香港占中运动被中共当局抓捕而维权；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年，曾因丈夫发表《修宪公民建议书》，提出删除“宪法序言”等政治改革建议，而被北京市石景山警方以涉嫌“妨害公务罪”刑拘，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年被江苏省徐州市中级法院以“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，直至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年才刑满获释，遂其为寻求正义而为丈夫身陷囹圄不断呼吁和维权；然而因其为夫维权发声被中共当局视为需要监控和打压的维稳对象，故而频遭当局骚扰和虐待；后在众多维权律师、正义人士及维权公民的鼎力支持、帮助下，以及在德国驻华大使馆官员和欧盟驻中国代表团等的关注、呼吁下，最终度过其人生中最艰困的时刻，并与被囚<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年刑满出狱的丈夫得以团聚；<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，因余文生许艳夫妇二人受邀参加欧盟驻华代表团座谈会见，在前往会见的途中被北京市石景山八角派出所警方拦截传唤，后即失联；<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，其夫妇均被石景山区警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘，家遭查抄；同年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，其二人又被以同罪名转正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，余文生代理律师到看守所要求与其会见遭到拒绝，随后被告知余文生涉罪又被新增“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月初获悉，余文生及其妻子许艳被从北京转至苏州关押，目前余文生关押于苏州市第一看守所，许艳关押于同地点的苏州市第四看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，许艳案开庭，<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日宣判，许艳被以“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。目前已经刑满获释，回到家中。</span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk189095637;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183794101;"><b _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk189095637;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183794101;"><span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日被抓捕后遣返中国大陆。后被以“组织他人偷越国境罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月。沈绍春牧师的父母都是基督教的传道人，其早年即皈依基督教，就读神学院，<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年开始全职传教，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年在缅甸佤邦创办“活水小学”。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年，其<span lang="EN-US">4</span>名在校上课的学生被缅甸当局抓捕移交中方，其随后也被抓捕，并移交中方。后被“组织他人偷越国境罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。刑期原本至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月提前<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月获释，此前前羁押在云南西双版纳的监狱中。</span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk189095637;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183794101;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，蚌埠活石归正教会的牧师万长春被安徽省蚌埠市公安局禹会分局以“涉嫌非法经营罪<span lang="EN-US">"</span>刑事拘留。随后，薛少强长老、万春琴同工，还有另外一个基督徒也以相同的罪名先后被刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，又被更改罪名，蚌埠经禹会区人民检察院批准，蚌埠禹会分局以“诈骗罪”对他们批捕。安徽省蚌埠市活石归正教会万长春、薛少强、曹斌挺、万春琴四名基督徒被控诈骗罪一案至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日一审庭审结束，除万长春仍在押，万春琴、薛少强、曹斌挺<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人均已取保候审回家，他们结束了一年八个月的被囚生活。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p _Hlk183794101;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、薛少强：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk189095637;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183794101;"><span _Hlk183794101;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">29</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk189095637;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183794101;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、刘汉斌：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk189095637;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183794101;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">重庆自媒体人，网名：文艺犯。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，刘汉斌因公开声援内蒙古清河县失地农民维权，被内蒙古呼和浩特警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”跨省抓捕，并被刑事拘留，目前关押在呼和浩特市第一看守所。律师提出取保候审的请求，于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日被呼和浩特警方以“案件重大复杂”为由拒绝，并且限制律师的正常会见权利。刘汉斌是一名长期关注社会问题、敢于揭露真相的自媒体人。他通过个人平台记录和揭露中国基层社会的不公现象，特别是失地农民的困境。此次事件的起因是刘汉斌公开支持内蒙古清河县失地农民的维权行动，揭露当地政府强行征地、补偿不足等问题。这些失地农民多年来上访未果，甚至遭到地方政府的暴力打压和非法拘禁。<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日刘汉斌已取保获释回家。<b>信息来源：</b></span></span></span></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2025/01/blog-post_89.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk189095637;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183794101;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2025/01/blog-post_89.html</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk189095637;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183794101;"></span></span></span></span></span></a><span _Hlk183794101;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></p><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk189095637;"></span><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183794101;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">30</span></b></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183794101;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、李宜雪：</span></b></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183794101;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">江西维权人士，女。李宜雪女士维权事件源于其在<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日遭派出所辅警猥亵，并在向警方指控后，竟然被警方送至江西省精神病院强制入院<span lang="EN-US">56</span>日的事件。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，南昌市公安局西湖分局发通报回应，认定涉事辅警赖某吉不存在猥亵行为，并指李宜雪在<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月中先后<span lang="EN-US">4</span>次在公共场合扬言自杀、自称患有抑郁症、难以入睡，丁公路派出所因此将其送至江西省精神病院，医院诊断后收治入院，民警也于当日通知家属。李宜雪后以医疗损害责任纠纷为由起诉江西省精神病院，并在网上曝光遭遇、发视频回应通报。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，诉江西省精神病院案一审开庭，庭审约两个小时，法院宣布择期宣判。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，李宜雪发布两则短视频称西湖分局筷子巷派出所所长带十余人闯入家中并破坏门口监控设备，此后李宜雪失联，引发网民持续关注。西湖区委宣传部<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日通报称，当地小区此后每日上门关心，李宜雪一直在家中。大批中国大陆网民尝试多种方式联系李宜雪未果。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，南昌市公安局西湖分局、西湖区南浦街道办事处发布通告称，<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日夜间北京安定医院<span lang="EN-US">3</span>名专家（另<span lang="EN-US">5</span>名民警、<span lang="EN-US">1</span>名小区干部陪同）已在协商后上门到李宜雪家中为李宜雪鉴定，并与李宜雪父亲谈话，<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日北京安定医院作出李宜雪患有强迫性障碍、人格障碍，鉴于李宜雪当前病情，<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日已将其送诊。上述公告并未打消公众质疑，相反，大陆民间舆论对中共当局再次强制将李宜雪关进精神病院一事表达强烈的不满，谴责之声一夜之间如海啸一般。后迫于舆论压力，<a name="_Hlk189096038">李宜雪</a>被释放回家。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183794101;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/12/blog-post_23.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><span _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">华秀珍、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><a name="_Hlk189092690"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1/</span></b></a></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk189092690;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">冯勇军</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">1973</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日出生，四川省绵阳市三台县人，原三台县百顷镇黄龙村二组<span lang="EN-US">023</span>号村民，现成都市金牛区金周路长住居民，实名举报人，人称“锦旗哥”，维权公民，中国在押维权人士。因冯勇军平素为人品行正直，凡其村中所遇不公之事均敢直言，以维护自己及村民的权益，故而颇得村民好评和认可，但却被村领导视为极好管闲事者而颇遭忌恨和报复性打压；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日<span lang="EN-US">-11</span>日，曾因对村中外包养鱼的百顷水库被严重污染而不满，并就申请村里水库承包合同公开、水库资金流向等问题向当地政府提起多项行政诉讼以寻求救济而无果，而与<span lang="EN-US">9</span>位村民联合给三台县环保局和三台县百顷镇党委政府各送一面“不作为”锦旗，以示警示，遂被三台县警方以涉嫌“扰乱社会秩序罪”刑拘，并送三台县看守所关押；获释后，又因不服当地警方处罚决定，而曾实名举报三台县公安局<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日处置送“不作为”锦旗事件违法违规，以期公安部及四川省公安厅指令绵阳市警方调查处理，但结局却是绵阳市警方以情况汇报系工作秘密、国家机密、国家绝密为由而拒不告知；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日<span lang="EN-US">-2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，曾因多次举报被警方非法限制人身自由和成都市青羊区警方行政不作为，并向青羊区法院提起诉讼，而被该法院以“属于刑事案件，不属于人民法院审查范围”为由作出多份行政裁定书，不予受理；后其被逼无奈，就多次持续报警并通过新浪微博声讨青羊区警方的不作为，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，遂被成都市青羊区警方以“扰乱单位秩序”为由处行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">14</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，因冯勇军第<span lang="EN-US">10</span>次来到四川高院蜀汉路办公区据悉投诉维权，而被成都市郫都区警方再次扣押，后被以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，被成都市郫都区检察院以同罪名正式批捕；据悉，其已给其妻子亲笔留言要求帮请律师。被羁押于成都市新都区看守所。后获悉冯勇军被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，被转监到成都市锦江监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2025/01/4_30.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2025/01/4_30.html</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2/</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">毛善春简介：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">1974</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日出生，湖北省公安县人，武汉市汉南区绿地协子河畔小区常驻居民，网络活跃人士，秦永敏中国人权观察团队成员，维权公民，民主异见人士，中国在押政治犯。早在<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年，毛善春曾因坚持捍卫法律尊严，依中华人民共和国宪法第<span lang="EN-US">35</span>条、第<span lang="EN-US">42</span>条、第<span lang="EN-US">27</span>条相关授权，捍卫个体基本人权，监督政府依法行政，保障公民合法权益，遂其积极参与中国人权观察的发起活动，并于次年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月受全体发起人委托，依法前往北京民政部社会组织注册厅申请注册；然而，历经<span lang="EN-US">4</span>次注册而未果，故其自此一直以该组织团队成员进行活动；后因在参与和经历多起维权事件的过程中，例如亲历过山东曲阜（薛福顺死亡）事件，黑龙江建三江事件，围观过河南郑州三看事件，湖南衡阳赵枫生颠覆案开庭，以及广州看守所张六毛死亡事件等等，遂其维权思想日趋成熟，更坚定地认知到法治民主才是社会发展进步的根本；然而，因其坚定的民主维权意识及行为，其长期受到地方当局及警方的骚扰和非法扣留等打压，并曾遭遇山东省曲阜市秘密机构无故殴打至鼻梁骨折，迄今仍未治愈；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，因其公开发表《关于退出中国共产党的声明》，致网络浏览流量和点赞量剧增，故其做法引发地方当局极为不快；<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，湖北省两会开幕之际，其因政府所谓「敏感时期」而被迫从武汉市返回老家公安县过年，不料竟于次日（<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日）被公安县警方以涉嫌「寻挑衅滋事罪」刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，又以同罪由转正式逮捕；同年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，其案被公安县警方移交至公安县检察院审查起诉；<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，其寻偿滋事罪案在湖北省公安县法院开庭受理，后获悉其一审获刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日；据悉，其在看守所内常遭精神折磨，且每次均达<span lang="EN-US">1</span>小时（或以上）；而其父亲因在其被抓捕之后有国保警方向其家属恐吓，称其涉嫌颠覆国家政权等罪名，故其父听到后心理悲愤交加，不幸过世。目前毛善春被羁押于湖北省公安县看守所。</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2025/01/4_23.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2025/01/4_23.html</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">3/</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈品霖简介</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">：网名<span lang="EN-US">Plato</span>，白纸运动《乌鲁木齐中路》记录片制作人。生于<span lang="EN-US">1991</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，福建省霞浦县人。在习近平政府推行疯狂清零政策三年期间，中国人民的日常生活和自由遭受到严重的侵害。而新疆乌鲁木齐发生的一场大火彻底将民众对防疫政策的不满点燃。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，当上海人民自发的聚集街头悼念火灾中逝去的同胞时，没人料到这场悼念活动将引发全国范围內对防疫政策的抗议。陈品霖在上海现场拍摄大量视频、制作了《乌鲁木齐中路》纪录片，纪录片再现了民众自发参加悼念乌鲁木齐火灾遇难者，进而演变为要求解封并提出政治诉求的“白纸运动”的过程和场面。陈品霖在白纸运动一周年之际（<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月下旬）将纪录片上传到网络，不到一周，于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，即遭抓捕，而其推特和<span lang="EN-US">Youtube</span>频道被销号。据悉与其一同被抓还有一位女生，后女生获取保，但陈品霖遭遭刑事拘留，后于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日被上海市公安局宝山分局以“涉嫌寻衅滋事罪”被正式批捕，于<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日被移送检察院审查起诉。陈品霖案已于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日由上海市宝山区检察院向上海市宝山区法院提起公诉。根据起诉书，陈品霖于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日晚在上海乌鲁木齐中路用手机拍摄并保存“<span lang="EN-US">11.26</span>”事件现场视频资料，于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月开始制作《乌鲁木齐中路》白纸运动一周年完整回顾纪录片，于<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日制作完成，通过多个境外平台推广，其中推特浏览量达<span lang="EN-US">21</span>万次。被指控“明知是编造的虚假信息，在信息网络上散布，造成公共秩序严重混乱；转发引用辱骂国家领导人言论，损害国家形象、严重危害国家利益”。<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日一审在上海宝山区法院开庭，后遭判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。陈品霖现被羁押在上海宝山区看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2025/01/plato36.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2025/01/plato36.html</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">4/</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">邓燕祥简历：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">1980</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">年代出生，广东省人，佛山市顺德区公民，基督徒，基督教全职侍奉同工，广东顺德盛佳家庭教会传道人，中国在押良心犯。早期曾为经商人，后因皈依基督教而将精力和爱好全心转投到教会的各项服侍活动中；又因为人和善、待人极有爱心，故其在顺德盛佳教会全职服侍的<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年间，曾帮助过许多对面临婚姻解体的基督徒夫妻，深得教会同工及教友信任与喜爱；但自近年来，因中共当局加强了对宗教事务条例的管理及修订，其所在盛佳教会频繁被当地民宗局要求加入和接受中共所属的“三自教会”的管理，被其等多次拒绝，遂屡被地方民宗局及顺德区警方的上门骚扰和警告；<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，盛佳教会突遭顺德区警方、民宗局和小区人员等数十人的连手冲击，教会使用的计算机、桌椅及教学物品等被翻查，教会大门被查封，邓燕祥、朱龙江、王伟才、朱巧玲<span lang="EN-US">4</span>名教会同工被警方带走；次日（<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日），其<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人均被顺德区警方以涉嫌“非法经营罪”刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，邓燕祥等<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人又被佛山市顺德区检察院以同罪名正式批捕，指控其等因让信徒使用教会印刷的内部学习数据，而此行为和思想意识与国家新修订的宗教管理条例相违背，故应予以逮捕、法办；被抓捕至今，其等均无更多具体信息，只知其等家属及孩子的生活、工作和上学正面临极大压力，教会其余未抓捕的同工和信徒仍遭警方持续传唤约谈；据悉，教会信徒均表示，因他们参与的家庭教会受到中国“宗教自由白皮书”保护，故而教会自己印刷内部学习数据并不违法。<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，盛佳教案宣判，邓燕祥传道被判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，刑期到<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，邓燕祥仍被羁押在南海区看守所。其余<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人王伟才、朱龙江、朱巧玲、朱龙飞被判<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>个月到<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月，目前均已获释。目前被羁押于佛山市南海区看守所（广东省佛山市南海区狮山镇招大（管理区）兴业东路，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">528200</span>）。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日华秀珍、谭华母女到浙江省政府上访后均被刑拘，<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日华秀珍被批捕，七月因严重高血压和房颤等危重病情转入监管医院，至今不认罪不认罚，公安不给家属拘留和批捕通知，看守所扣押家属信件，后获悉华秀珍女士因退休金被当局非法克扣而上访再遭判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，狱中期间遭迫害病危收入监管医院。女儿谭华于<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日探视，华秀珍已卧床不起，四目相交，眼泪喷涌。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span Roman&quot;;">2</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New
