_Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张展、廉长年、廉旭亮、付娟、徐秦、何方美、季孝龙、李怀庆、张春雷、张忠顺、管晓燕、孙承浩等<span lang="EN-US">12</span>人狱中动态信息通报：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1/</span></b></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张展<span lang="EN-US">:</span>遭羁押整整<span lang="EN-US">5</span>个月的著名人权捍卫者<a name="_Hlk189026618">张展</a>女士狱中再次绝食抗争，被看守所强迫灌食<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，本网获悉：遭羁押整整<span lang="EN-US">5</span>个月的著名人权捍卫者张展女士狱中再次绝食抗争，被看守所强迫灌食。强迫灌食的过程，以及剥夺适足医疗照护，均足以构成违反《禁止酷刑公约》的残忍与不人道待遇，且该公约早已被中国批准。本网敦促浦东看守所立即停止强迫灌食！张展女士曾获刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，去年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月才刑满出狱。出狱<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月后，即<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，张展因营救被抓捕的甘肃青年民主活动人士张盼成，从上海只身赴甘肃，说服张母签署了委托书。后其回到老家陕西咸阳，于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日在当地被上海警方带回上海，后遭当局以涉嫌寻衅滋事罪刑事拘留，后经浦东新区检察院批准，上海市公安局浦东分局于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日以涉嫌寻衅滋事罪对张展女士正式执行逮捕。目前张展被羁押在浦东新区看守所。张展被抓捕后，引起国际社会的高度关注。当局仍然以各种方式封锁张展案的信息，使得张展案件细节无法被外界所知晓。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张展简历：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1983</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日出生，陕西省咸阳市人，上海市浦东新区居民，曾任职于上海市某证券公司高管，原执业律师，公民记者，人权捍卫者，中国在押政治犯。早期，曾就读于西南财经大学金融专业并获取硕士学位；自<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年起，离开家乡到上海谋职；曾为追求自由理想而甘愿放弃在一家证券公司的高薪职位；曾任职律师，但后因在网上发表针砭时弊的文章而遭报复，被迫离开律师岗位；因不满中共当局的政治现状，曾长期在网络平台发表批评“一党专政”、腐败滥权等言论，且因内容尖锐，颇具针对性，而被上海警方多次约谈、传唤及威胁；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年以来，因在微信等社交软件上大量转发香港“反送中”抗议视频及文图资料，尤其是在上海街头举伞要求结束社会主义制度、共产党下台等，随于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日被上海市黄浦区警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘，期间曾被两次做强制性“精神病鉴定”，至<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日才准予取保候审释放；自<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年初以来，曾因武汉冠状病毒疫情蔓延，其为了获取一手数据，不惧风险，亲赴武汉做实地疫情考察与报导；此举很快遭到中共当局的极端不满和迅速打压；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，被武汉警方从一家暂住旅店抓走，次日被上海市浦东新区警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，被浦东新区检察院予以批捕；<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，其案被移送至上海市浦东新区法院；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，被该法院一审以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日；据悉，其家属要求探监曾长期遭拒；其因狱中长期绝食抗议，被强行灌食，致其身体情况十分虚弱。此前张展一直在上海市女子监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，因赴甘肃营救张盼成，再遭当局抓捕，被刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日被正式批捕。目前羁押在浦东看守所。</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2025/01/5_25.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2025/01/5_25.html</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2/3/4/</span></b></span></span></span><a name="_Hlk189028128"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">廉长年、廉旭亮、付娟</span></b></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：西安丰盛教会教案将于<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日在西安市灞桥区人民法院召开庭前会议<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，本网获悉：西安丰盛教会教案将于<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日在西安市灞桥区人民法院召开庭前会议。西安丰盛教会牧师、传道人廉长年、廉旭亮、付娟，自<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被控“诈骗罪”被羁押至今。廉长年牧师在看守所度过了<span lang="EN-US">70</span>岁生日，他年迈的身体在高强内艰难的环境中也日渐衰弱。他们<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人先被指定居所监视居住<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，期间均被酷刑；<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，三人被以涉嫌诈骗罪刑拘。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月底他们的案子已进入法院，起诉金额为<span lang="EN-US">39</span>万元，三人被检方均求刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。西安丰盛教会自成立三十年以来，严格遵行《圣经》教导，未曾有人以被牧者诈辦为由报案，此教案纯属冤枉陷害。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">廉长年简介<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">河南省人，基督徒，原河南“中华福音团契”（中国五大家庭教会之一）老一辈牧者，西安丰盛基督教教会创建人，主任牧师。上世纪<span lang="EN-US">90</span>年代廉长年牧师在西安市建立了丰盛基督教教会；但自<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月中共新《宗教事务条例》正式生效实施起，全国各地基督教家庭教会纷纷遭遇空前严打和迫害，其所建西安丰盛教会亦遭严打和冲击；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年，自<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日始，其教会信徒突遭西安市灞桥区十里铺派出所警方大规模口头传唤和上门问讯，甚至有些人家被多次搜查，旨在胁迫信徒们作证，控告牧师诈骗和传播邪教，甚至要求信徒捏造有关教会奉献的虚假信息；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，其及妻子、儿子、儿媳以及教会同工等<span lang="EN-US">6</span>人被当地派出所警方强行带走并被抄家，次日，其父子二人和教会财务同工付娟等人被西安市灞桥区警方以涉嫌“诈骗罪”指定居所监视居住；后遭刑事拘留、逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，其教会被西安市民政局迅速发布通告取缔，理由是其与“中华福音总会”、“中华福音总会”西安区联会，“未经登记”就擅自以社会团体名义开展活动，故被认定为非法社会组织；其案虽已有多名维权律师介入，但其等<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人曾被长期秘押，警方一直以当事人案情涉及危害国家安全为由拒绝律师会见。现案件已经到法院，检察院以诈骗罪对其求刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2025/01/202527.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2025/01/202527.html</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">5/</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">徐秦：获刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年的江苏人权捍卫者徐秦女士已被转监至南京女子监狱<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，本网获悉：近日，获刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年的江苏人权捍卫者徐秦女士已被转监至南京女子监狱服刑。收件地址：南京女子监狱（南京市雨花台区凤信路<span lang="EN-US">28</span>号）狱政科转徐秦， 邮编<span lang="EN-US">210012 </span>，电话<span lang="EN-US">025-52353911</span>。徐秦患有高血压、冠心病、脑梗、腔梗，看守所期间被拒绝保外就医。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，徐秦在其被羁押近<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年半后，经过<span lang="EN-US">12</span>次延期审理，被以“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”一审判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。其不服判决，依法上诉，二审维持原判。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">徐秦简历：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1962</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>出生，江苏省高邮市高邮县人，先做过供销社工人，社区街道办事处工作人员，中共曾经党员，基督徒。民间维权组织“中国人权观察”前秘书长，“玫瑰团队”成员，人权捍卫者，中国在押政治犯。长期以来，一直关注中国人权状况，并与著名人权活动家、民主异议人士秦永敏一道筹建中国人权观察；自秦永敏被捕、秦之妻子赵素利“被失踪”后，她曾次上街声援，跟进案件；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，被警方突然限制自由，之后一直遭跟踪与监控；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，其在从扬州高邮到昆山的途中被警方带走，后得知其被扬州市警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，其家属委托的代理律师要求会见，遭到警方拒绝，但被告知其已于<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日由刑拘转为“指定居所监视居住”；<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，又被追加罪名，以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”继续扣留，且不准律师会见；据悉，此次被捕，皆与其近年来坚持关注人权问题，后又积极组织联署声援维权律师余文生，以及为维权公民徐琳筹款等活动有关；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日获悉，其已获取保释放；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，徐秦突然又被警方从家中带走；据悉，之前其案件一直处于延审中；此次被捕前，徐秦刚做完心脏搭桥手术，且患有脑梗、心梗、高血压等多种疾病。狱中身体状况急剧恶化，甚至瘫痪无法站立。后在律师的抗争和各界关注下，徐秦身体比以前好了一些，在别人的搀扶下可以走一小会。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月份看守所安排她到东方医院做了检查，开了一些药。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日徐秦案已经在扬州市看守所法庭召开庭前会议，但长时间仍不开庭审理。徐秦案被延期审理竟然达到十二次，中共政权玩弄法律的肆无忌惮，令世人叹为观止。徐秦案终于在<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日上午于扬州市中级人民法院开庭宣判，法庭判决徐秦犯煽动颠覆国家政权罪，处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。其不服判决依法上诉，二审维持原判。此前徐秦被羁押于江苏省扬州市看守所，现转监至南京女子监狱。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2025/01/4_14.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2025/01/4_14.html</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">6/</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">何方美：获刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月“的疫苗宝宝之家”发起人、著名人权捍卫者何方美女士二审维持原判 两个女儿仍被强迫失踪<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，本网获悉：获刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月的“疫苗宝宝之家”发起人、著名人权捍卫者何方美二审维持原判，两个女儿仍被强迫失踪。近日，何方美案二审由河南省新乡市中级人民法院裁定：驳回上诉，维持原判。新乡中院以重婚罪可以公诉，以及何方美为疫苗致残女儿维权、泼墨政府是寻衅滋事的理由，维持了一审有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月的判决。本案中对未成年人的迫害尤其残酷：自<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，何方美的两个幼女一直被关押在监视居住的新乡辉县共济医院。自<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月初，新乡辉县当局转移两个幼女至未知地点，拒不告诉任何亲属，多名亲属多方苦寻幼女至今无果。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">何方美简介：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">“疫苗宝宝之家”发起人、著名人权捍卫者。何方美与李新夫妇原本健康的女儿<span lang="EN-US">1</span>岁<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月时在河南省新乡市辉县接种问题疫苗后，突发病毒性急性脊髓炎，自此残疾。何方美为女儿奔走维权，创办“疫苗宝宝之家”，联合别的疫苗受害者及家人维权，乃至于到辉县政府门前泼墨抗议。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，孕妇何方美带着时年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>岁的儿子、<span lang="EN-US">3</span>岁的残障女儿，被辉县市公安局以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”指定居所监视居住在新乡市共济医院，家属未得到通知。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月，何方美在共济医院指定居所监视居住期间，产下小女儿。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，何方美被辉县市公安局以涉嫌寻衅滋事等罪执行逮捕，被羁押于河南省新乡市看守所至今。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，何方美的辩护律师介入后，才知何方美的案件一审已经开过庭，但办案单位未通知何方美亲属；李新已被判刑五年，在河南焦作监狱服刑；其子被辉县市政府送至村民家里寄养；两幼女继续被关在共济医院。律师向辉县市法院主张阅卷和重新开庭，均被拒绝。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月开始，何方美家属去共济医院还能偶尔探视俩女孩。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年夏天，俩女孩被关进有电子锁的病区，家人们无法正常探视，只能通过护工偶尔获知女孩近况，辗转送物资。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，律师向新乡市中级人民法院提出控告，才于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月获许阅卷。目前，该案一审开庭两年多，迟迟不下判长达<span lang="EN-US">30</span>个月。作为母亲的何方美非常担心孩子们的生活、身心健康情况、受教育状况，希望早日出来照顾、陪伴孩子。她和李新的儿子被政府安排寄养村民家，两个女儿——<span lang="EN-US">7</span>岁的希希（化名）和<span lang="EN-US">3</span>岁的娇娇（化名）——也于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年清明节前被转移至它处，目前下落不明。亲属非常担忧两个小女孩的安全。自<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>被抓捕羁押，至今已超过<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，辉县法院在新乡看守所一审宣判何方美案，何方美被以重婚罪、寻衅滋事罪，判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。何方美自<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月起被监视居住长达<span lang="EN-US">18</span>个月，本案<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月一审开庭后，迟迟不下判长达<span lang="EN-US">30</span>个月。而其两个年幼女儿目前仍然下落不明。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/10/456.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/10/456.html</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">7/</span></b></span></span></span><a name="_Hlk189031650"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">季孝龙</span></b></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：上海提篮桥监狱剥夺人权捍卫者季孝龙的亲情会见权<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，本网获悉：上海人权捍卫者季孝龙自<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日转至上海提篮桥监狱服刑至今，其家属一直被禁止探视。季孝龙家属曾电话询问狱方，狱方以季孝龙不肯会见为由拒绝家属探视。但实际上，监狱每月安排服刑犯人进行亲情会见，属于例行程序，并不需要征求犯人意见，也没有犯人会在与世隔绝的监狱中拒绝亲人的探视。季孝龙是在<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月被二审维持原判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月的刑期，随后转到上海新收犯监狱进行所谓“培训”，再于<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日转到上海提篮桥监狱正式开始服刑。季孝龙的父亲曾于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月到提篮桥监狱要求探视，被监狱方拒绝。此后多次电话询问狱方，均被搪塞推诿，再后狱方一听到询问有关季孝龙的电话就直接挂断。按正常程序，犯人下监后一个月内，监狱就应安排亲属探视。上海提篮桥监狱长期剥夺季孝龙亲情会见权，并以季孝龙本人不肯会见为由拒绝家属探视，理由荒唐，只能说明季孝龙在上海提篮桥监狱遭到了非人的特别对待，监狱不敢让季孝龙的真实状况被家属看到。此前有信息传出，季孝龙在提蓝桥监狱<span lang="EN-US">11</span>监区被单独关押，而单独关押属于禁闭，是一种对犯人的惩罚措施。因此，季孝龙在上海提篮桥监狱的境况堪忧。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">季孝龙简介：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">1976</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日出生，江苏省张家港市人，张家港市杨舍镇名都花苑居民，基督徒，民主人士，人权捍卫者，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，曾因宣传民主理念而被上海市浦东新区警方以“寻衅滋事”罪由传唤，并被处以行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，曾因在网上发文，呼吁民主人士响应“厕所革命”，并在医院、大学等公共场所的厕所门上，用马克笔写宣传语“大病治不起，习胖狂撒币，修宪妄称帝、苦难何时毕！打倒共产党。还政于民，结束民众苦难。推翻习核心，拒走文革路”等字句，短时间内响应者众多，随于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日被浦东新区警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留；同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，又被送到指定居所监视居住；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，被以同罪由转正式逮捕，关押在上海市浦东新区看守所。羁押期间，警方曾多次以让其“死亡”和用寒冷气温逼迫其认罪，致其身体虚弱发病吐血；其家属曾送羽绒服和《圣经》书籍遭拒收。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，其案被上海市浦东新区检察院起诉至上海市浦东新区法院；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，最终被该法院以“寻衅滋事罪”一审判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。后送上海市白茅岭监狱七监区服刑，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日刑满获释。服刑期间遭到虐待。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年季孝龙出狱时正值疫情。在当年上海封城期间，其为上海市民持续发声，在互联网上公开发表《速停运动式防疫，纾困解难发救济》请命书，要求当局停止运动式防疫措施，向时任上海市委书记、现任总理的李强进行实名问责，要求其下台并承担重大事故责任。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，再次被上海市梅园新村派出所警察从家中带走，后被上海市浦东新区警方以“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，被浦东新区检察院以同罪名正式批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，季孝龙一审被以寻衅滋事罪判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，公诉方以他在推特上公开批评国家领导人作为罪证。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月二审秘密开庭，<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月上海市第一中级法院终审维持原判。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年，季孝龙获得当年度的“青年中国人权奖”。季孝龙目前服刑于上海市提篮桥监狱，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2025/01/blog-post_17.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2025/01/blog-post_17.html</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">8/</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李怀庆：获刑<span lang="EN-US">20</span>年的重庆民营企业家李怀庆在贵州省兴义监狱内因营养不良导致其健康状况恶化<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，本网获悉：获刑<span lang="EN-US">20</span>年的重庆民营企业家李怀庆在贵州省兴义监狱内因营养不良导致其健康状况恶化。李怀庆妻子包艳今天通报：李怀庆在贵州省兴义监狱内因营养不良和环境导致其健康恶化。由于监狱缺乏必要的食物供应，李怀庆的胃部出现问题。李怀庆在监狱服刑，其生存权和健康权应该得到保障。我呼吁立即改善监狱的饮食和卫生条件，提供足够的营养支持。重庆民营企业家、亿万富翁李怀庆，因在微信上说几句话，就被当局以煽动颠覆国家政权，及诈骗、敲诈勒索、非法拘禁等四项罪名羁押。在被关押近三年之后，于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日在重庆市第一中级法院宣判，获刑<span lang="EN-US">20</span>年，令世人震惊。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李怀庆简历：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">1966</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日出生，重庆市人，复转军人，“随手公益”的志愿者，重庆富华典当公司老板，民营企业家，中国在押政治犯。因个性急公好义，曾长期关注和资助弱势群体；曾因默默多年资助大凉山地区贫困儿童及家境困难的昔日战友，积极参与“大爱清尘”活动救助尘肺病工友，并为此先后捐资近<span lang="EN-US">30</span>万元，不计回报，而深受弱势群体爱戴欢迎；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，被重庆市警方突然以“涉黑” 罪名刑拘，其妻儿及公司职员等亦受牵连被抓，在被莫名其妙数时小时审讯、恐吓、威逼之后才得释放；同年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月，其名下公司、妻子包艳及与此案完全无关的其胞姊资产、账户（包括现金及房产等，总值上亿元）均被重庆警方以“打黑”名义冻结；后其罪名被重庆市检察院更换为涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”，指控其在<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月—<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月，曾七度在微信“以造谣、诽谤等方式煽动颠覆国家政权”，包括转发“红四方面军在四川杀人百万”文章，又转发过有“道义抗争”、“暴力革命”等字眼的录音，属于违法行为；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，其罪名遂于“涉黑罪”变成“颠覆国家政权罪”；在其长达近两年的羁押过程中，其律师及其家属均未收到过任何有关其涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”的逮捕通知书或文件说明；后李怀庆涉嫌煽动颠覆国家政权罪案于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日在重庆市第一中级法院开庭审理，未宣判。目前李怀庆被羁押于重庆江北区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日重庆民营企业家李怀庆被庆市第一中级法院以煽动颠覆国家政权罪、诈骗罪、敲诈勒索罪、非法拘禁罪四项罪名判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">20</span>年徒刑。后被关押在贵州省六盘水市六盘水监狱。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月又被转监到贵州省兴义监狱。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2025/01/20.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2025/01/20.html</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">9/</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张春雷：获刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年的贵阳仁爱归正教会张春雷长老狱中情况通报：<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月第一次会见妻子<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，本网获悉：据张春雷长老妻子杨爱清师母：“今天上午（<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日），时隔三年十个月，见到了春雷。感谢神，春雷很健康，也很喜乐，通话的半个小时中，春雷说得最多的是要喜乐，并充满感恩，神所量给他的环境，都是神的恩赐，春雷说不要怨恨任何人，上帝的恩典天天同在。对那些错判他的人，要更多为他们祷告。请大家放心，他很好，春雷向大家问安。”<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><a name="_Hlk189055894"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张春雷</span></b></a></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">简历：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">1964</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月出生<span lang="EN-US">, </span>贵州省人，基督徒，贵阳市仁爱归正家庭教会主要组建人，教会带领人、长老，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年《牧者联署：为基督信仰的声明》首批签名人之一，中国在押良心犯。早年，曾因笃信耶稣基督，为广传基督教福音而与人共同组建了不从中共“三自教会”的“仁爱归正教会”；起初，该教会仅有几十会众，但在其不懈努力和事工（即神职人员在教会里所做的服务）带领下，因能热情广泛接待南来北往的信徒，故而在后来的国度事工中起到和发挥了重要的作用；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年，曾因积极参与由四川成都王怡牧师发起的《牧者联署：为基督信仰的声明》的首批联署签名，随遭贵阳当局的严管监控；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，其教会被贵阳市南明区民族宗教事务局突然取缔，并被指称，因其等一行人“未经批准，擅自以‘仁爱归正教会’名义在南明区中天商务港设立宗教场所，组织、举行宗教活动，接受宗教性捐献，违反《宗教事务条例》相关规定，责令停止宗教活动，拆除相关设施和标识”，最终致使其及教会信徒在失去会堂后只能在餐厅、酒店进行主日敬拜；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年，曾因在当地某酒店举行主日聚会，而被数十名宗教局人员及警方先后<span lang="EN-US">3</span>次连手冲击，<span lang="EN-US">2</span>次被封门，敬拜所用的十字架被强摘，其计算机等用品被查收；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，曾因其教会新租房屋的房东再次被当局威胁，故而其被逼无奈只得再次从新租的房屋搬走；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，因其教会有十数名信众在参加小组学习时被突然闯入的贵阳市南明区民宗局人员和警方带走，遂其赶到派出所与警方交涉要人，不料竟遭粗暴野蛮对待，并被以“非法经营社团”为由处行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">11</span>天；拘留期满时，又被贵阳市云岩区警方以涉嫌“诈骗罪”刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，被贵阳市云岩区检察院以同罪名正式批捕；据悉，其妻子、儿子受牵连曾遭警方长时讯问且其妻遭虐待，教会多位同工成员亦遭抄家；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日—<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，其代理律师数次要求会见均受阻，被告知其“因涉嫌危害国家安全，在侦查期间未得到办案单位允许的情况下，禁止律师会见”。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年初遭起诉。于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日开庭，未宣判张春雷长老被控“煽动颠覆国家政权罪、诈骗罪”一案于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日上午<span lang="EN-US">10:00</span>在贵州省贵阳市中级人民法院进行宣判，张春雷长被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。目前张春雷长老被羁押于贵阳市看守所。</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2025/01/5310.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">10/</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张忠顺：被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年半的“厦门公民聚会案”当事人、人权捍卫者<a name="_Hlk189055990">张忠顺</a>已被收押进山东省济滕监狱<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，本网近日获悉：被以“颠覆国家政权罪”、“私藏枪支弹药罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月的“厦门公民聚会案”当事人、人权捍卫者张忠顺，已于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月被收押进山东省济滕监狱，正式开始服刑。目前家属仍未获会见。济滕监狱通信地址：山东省济南市济阳区孙耿街道六一农场<span lang="EN-US">0109</span>信箱，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">251408</span>；电话<span lang="EN-US">0531-55860861</span>目前在押服刑的“厦门公民聚会案”当事人中，许志永被判刑<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年，在山东省鲁南监狱服刑；丁家喜被判刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年，在湖北省江北监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张忠顺简介：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">1967</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日生，山东省蓬莱市人，人权捍卫者、复旦大学<span lang="EN-US">-</span>香港大学<span lang="EN-US">IMBA</span>毕业，烟台大学前教师，独立思想者，“<span lang="EN-US">12</span>·<span lang="EN-US">13</span>厦门聚会案”当事人。<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年在烟台大学经济与工商管理学院任教期间，因在课堂上讲授《公共伦理学》时引用<span lang="EN-US">1989</span>年六四事件视频，被学生家长举报，当年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被山东省烟台市莱山区警方秘密抓捕，家被查抄，<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，被以涉嫌邪教罪刑拘，并被送至济南武警总医院（济南新康监狱）关押；<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，被以涉嫌“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”逮捕，关押于烟台市看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，被烟台市莱山区法院以同罪名判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年；上诉后烟台市中级法院二审维持原判，同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日被送山东省监狱服刑；<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月出狱，<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月即被烟台大学开除公职，所住房子被强拆。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月上旬，许志永、丁家喜等<span lang="EN-US">20</span>余名维权律师和人权捍卫者在厦门聚会，张忠顺是参加者之一。为此，他于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被中共当局“<span lang="EN-US">12.13</span>专案组”以“颠覆国家政权”为名监视居住，近半年后获释。此后，因为给许志永、丁家喜的辩护律师出具证言，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，张忠顺第二次被山东烟台警方以同案同罪名监视居住，其住所再次遭到搜查。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，张忠顺被转押到山东临沂市临沭县看守所刑事拘留；<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月被临沂中级法院秘密开庭审理，法院事前未通知家属。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月被山东临沂中级法院以“颠覆国家政权罪”“私藏枪支弹药罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2025/01/4_7.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2025/01/4_7.html</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">11/</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">管晓燕：遭抓捕羁押的山东青岛女教师<a name="_Hlk189057375">管晓燕</a>女士案开庭已过半年多仍无判决结果<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，本网获悉：遭抓捕羁押的山东青岛女教师管晓燕案开庭已过半年多仍无判决结果。管晓燕系山东省青岛市即墨区一小学高级教师。因组织联署签名‘抵制警察肆意羁押维权人士’而被捕入狱，至今羁押已超过<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年半。其案件已于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>号在青岛第二看守所内开庭，因拒绝承诺放弃维权权利，被延期数次审理，半年过去，目前还无判决结果。管晓燕在<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日被关看守所前也因联署问题被关押医院监视居住达一年之久。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">管晓燕简历：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1966</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3.</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日出生，山东省青岛市即墨区开发区张家烟霞村人，小学高级教师。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月起，因抵抗强拆、上访被潮海派出所传唤、拘留多次。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月拘留期间两处房屋被拆。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月被截访控制人身自由，因高血压停药心脏病复发险些丧命。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月带头签署<span lang="EN-US">4</span>千人联名建议书，建议将限制人身自由的行政处罚权从公安移交至检察院，准备提交全国人大。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，即墨区山师实验学校领导王光迎询问联名建议书，劝管晓燕放弃维权，被拒。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日抓捕后关押在医院一年于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月取保候审。取保期间管晓燕依然不放弃利用网络在访民群体中进行普法活动，于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月份再次在网络访民群体开展题目为“金色的翅膀”的签名活动，准备将签名提交人大申请成立访民监督管理委员会。总签名人数达到一万一千八百多人，签名者提供身份证正反两面照片作为实名签名依据。签名活动受到关注后全国各地有访民陆陆续续被当地派出所民警找到做笔录。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日管晓燕被带走关押。据悉案件已于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>号在青岛第二看守所内开庭，尚无结果。目前管晓燕关押在青岛第二看守所（即墨市普东镇青平高速普东出口处），邮编<span lang="EN-US">266234</span>，电话<span lang="EN-US">0532-66578929</span>。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2025/01/blog-post_4.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2025/01/blog-post_4.html</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">12</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、<a name="_Hlk189021140">孙承浩：羁押至今<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年多仍未开庭。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></a></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk189021140;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">2023</span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk189021140;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">年<span lang="EN-US">12 </span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，甘肃省张掖市公安局却以涉嫌 “组织他人偷越国边境罪”刑事拘留孙承浩牧师，至今仍被羁押在张掖市甘州区看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk189021140;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">孙承浩</span></b></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">简历：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">甘肃张掖牧师。<span lang="EN-US">1982</span>年出生，是中国朝鲜族人，自幼跟随牧师父亲从东北移民到西北甘肃张掖传福音，耳濡目染父亲对上帝的敬畏及对失丧灵魂的关切，被上帝所呼召，年轻时就献身自己成为传道人。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月孙承浩牧师和朋友以正规途径（通过正规平台购买飞机票， 正常在海关出入境）赴韩国济州岛观光。济州岛一行孙承浩牧师自始至终没有跟任何人收取过任何费用，只是为方便大家沟通建了一个名为“济州岛自由行”的微信群，旅行结束后，所有人正常返回中国。但<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12 </span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，甘肃省张掖市公安局却以涉嫌“组织他人偷越国边境罪”刑事拘留孙承浩牧师，至今仍被羁押在张掖市甘州区看守所。孙承浩牧师被逮捕以后，妻女深受沉重打击，他们在张掖没有任何亲人，原教会的弟兄姐妹也都被约谈警告不准与他们联系，使他们的生活雪上加霜。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2025/01/blog-post_26.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2025/01/blog-post_26.html</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> </span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><a name="_Hlk189093691"></a><a name="_Hlk159649535"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk189093691;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">四、</span></b></span></a></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk189093691;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">本期新增被刑事拘留、被精神病的<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人名单及简历<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">：</span></span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk189093691;"><a name="_Hlk175805580"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175805580;"></span><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、庞光辉：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">男，<span lang="EN-US">1960</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日生，汉族，户籍地：辽宁省沈阳市大东区新东三街。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，庞光辉前往北京公安部上访，在途径唐山火车站时，被铁路民警以网络通缉逃犯身份扣押，后交由沈阳市公安局经济开发区公安分局押回沈阳。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，庞光辉再次被以寻衅滋事罪刑事拘留，直至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日被取保候审释放，同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日下午，在公园下象棋聊天时，被经济开发区公安分局带走并于次日<span lang="EN-US">(11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日<span lang="EN-US">)</span>刑事拘留，先羁押于铁西区看守所。后于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日以寻衅滋事罪批捕，目前羁押于沈阳市大东区看守所。庞光辉上访<span lang="EN-US">18</span>年没解决劳动争议主体诉求，却被不断打击报复，多次刑拘。<b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2025/01/blog-post_20.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2025/01/blog-post_20.html</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、曹可雄：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">四川自贡民主人士，网名雄心壮志，经了解，已确认曹可雄于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日再次被自贡市荣县旭阳派出所（电话<span lang="EN-US">0813-6201156</span>）送进自贡市第五人民医院（精神病医院）<span lang="EN-US">,</span>至今已经一月有余。曹可雄在<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日曾被荣县旭阳派出所（同上）送入自贡市第五人民医院（精神病院）（同上）强制“治疗”，直到<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日被释放，在精神病院有被电疗、强迫吃药。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">曹可雄父母均为体制内退休人员，他是家里独子，他本人是自贡高山镇卫生院预防接种科工作人员。曹可雄于<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>年出生，有泛蓝情节，是孙中山“三民主义”忠实拥护者，经常用多个微信号在朋友圈抨击时弊，为弱势群体发声，并因此多次被派出所以寻衅滋事罪名拘留。曹可雄<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月从精神病院释放后，曾和网友说明自己被强制治疗情况，并请求网友帮助解救另一位他了解到的、当时还被关在自贡精神病医院的异议人士涂强。曹可雄微信朋友曹可雄微信朋友圈在<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日停止更新。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2025/01/blog-post_16.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2025/01/blog-post_16.html</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">3</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、<a name="_Hlk189053171">姜卫东</a>：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">男，网名心无界，江苏灌云人，<span lang="EN-US">1983</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日出生。因在网络发表政治观点，行使议政权利，于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日以寻衅滋事罪名被灌云县公安局刑事拘留，经东海县人民检察院批准，于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日遭批捕，现关押江苏连云港市灌云县看守所（电话<span lang="EN-US">0518-88288657</span>，邮编<span lang="EN-US">222000</span>，具体地址：连云港市灌云县伊山镇任二庄）。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年姜卫东曾经和四川籍维权人士彭金元（网名子元）、湖南衡阳籍维权人士李增然在那年的深圳“保钓”大游行队伍中打出“民主、自由、人权、宪政”横幅而遭受传唤。姜卫东多年来，积极参与同城的各种民主维权活动和联署行动。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2025/01/blog-post_14.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2025/01/blog-post_14.html</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><a name="_Hlk189053488"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">4</span></b></a></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk189053488;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、费晓胜</span></b></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1968</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日出生，陕西省西安市人，基督徒，前上海市中国水墨美术馆执行馆长，前北京市本溪美术馆执行馆长及湘宁文化艺术机构艺术总监，北京市宋庄艺术区音乐人、艺术家，人称“宋庄音乐艺术圈老炮儿”，异议人士，中国在押政治犯。因其自幼喜欢艺术，故大学毕业后曾先在上海市八百号艺术区担任中国水墨美术馆执行馆长，数年后又转到北京<span lang="EN-US">798</span>艺术区，先后任职于本溪美术馆执行馆长和湘宁文化艺术机构艺术总监；之后，因其常年活动于北京宋庄艺术区，主要从事绘画、音乐策展以及行为艺术节等活动，故其作品深受会展参观者的欢迎，曾被美法英澳等多国的都市－如纽约、巴黎、伦敦等地的画廊和私人收藏；但因其为人正直、有正义感，不仅克己敬业于事业，也关心时事，故其曾在<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年因声援及支持香港反送中运动，而被中共警方拘留<span lang="EN-US">4 0</span>多天，且其护照亦被搜缴烧毁；自此，其对中国的国情和政治现状有了更多更深刻的认识；据悉，其之前曾已「走线」（指中国大陆居民为政治或经济原因，铤而走险非法移民至外国居住和工作的行为）出过国门，并用新办的护照到达了欧洲塞尔维亚，但之后其又大意回国办事；正当准备再次出国时，<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，其突然被西安市警方以不具名罪由带走、刑拘；对其突然被抓捕，消息一经传播，立引外界对中国文化圈“秋后算账”行动的极大关注，称其是自在押艺术家政治犯高兟之后又一位出国前夕被捕的艺术家。目前被羁押于西安碑林看守所（陕西省西安市长安区杜曲新村，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">710104</span>）。<b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2025/01/blog-post_71.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">五、</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，漯河市源汇区公安分局抓捕了杨俊成、丁香芹夫妇，并抄家。关押至漯河市第二看守所。后遭刑事拘留、批捕起诉。后获悉：杨俊成、丁香芹夫妻俩均被判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，杨俊成目前被关押在郑州新密监狱，丁香芹目前被关押在新乡女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2033</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" _Hlk178514727;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、丁香芹</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">：河南漯河市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">60</span>多岁，高中毕业后在工厂工作，<span lang="EN-US">30</span>多岁就因中共迫害失去工作流离失所并且无法办理身份证，二零零一年在劳教所受酷刑迫害牙齿几乎掉光。丈夫是杨俊成。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，漯河市源汇区公安分局抓捕了杨俊成、丁香芹夫妇，并抄家。关押至漯河市第二看守所。后遭刑事拘留、批捕起诉。后获悉：杨俊成、丁香芹夫妻俩均被判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，杨俊成目前被关押在郑州新密监狱，丁香芹目前被关押在新乡女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2033</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: lang="EN-US">3</span>日，李艳霞在武汉武昌区宝通寺宣讲法轮功时被人举告，被抓捕、关押在到武汉市第一看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年底，李艳霞被判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年。随即转监到武汉市宝丰路女子监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2032</span>年<span _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">湖北省随州市法轮功学员，女，家住湖北省随州市曾都区东城。她于一九九八年五月开始修炼法轮功。因坚持修炼法轮功，何卓君多次被中共抓捕、关押，在看守所、劳教所、洗脑班遭受迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日被随州市公安局国保支队、曾都分局国保大队警察抓捕，随即遭刑事拘留、后遭批捕、起诉；<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月被随州市曾都区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚款一万元。<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月初获悉：何卓君已于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被劫入武汉监狱关押迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2031</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">5</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">黑龙江省大庆市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1967</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月生，物业公司职工，家住黑龙江大庆市让胡路区东湖二区。她于一九九八年三月开始修炼法轮功，中共一九九九年七月开始疯狂迫害法轮功后，王正勇遭受多次骚扰和抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，大庆各公安分局警察在一天之内绑架了三十多名法轮功学员。当天中午，王正勇被闯入家中的警察抓捕到东湖分局，警察抄走她的法轮功书籍和等私人物品。当日下午五点多，王正勇被“取保候审”回家。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，东湖分局警察以取保候审到期为由，再次抓捕了王正勇，并与检察院将她构陷到让胡路区法院。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月开庭，后获悉其遭判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2031</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2025/01/7.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2025/01/7.html</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">6</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、何启明：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">1988</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日出生，英文名<span lang="EN-US">Kalvin Ho Kai-ming</span>，基督徒，原英属香港籍，香港新界东调景岭居住公民，前公民党成员，前香港民阵副召集人和前民主民生协进会（简称「民协」）副主席，原香港深水埗区议会南昌东选区议员，泛民主派人士，中国在押政治犯。早年，从香港基督教宣道会宣基中学毕业后，曾就读于香港城市大学，获取社会科学学士（公共政策与政治方向）学位后，又在中国神学研究院修读基督教研究硕士；曾于中学时代就加入公民党，后来又加入了民协，故其曾拥有公民党与民协双重党籍；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年，其退出公民党，转而关注于为民协做地区性工作，主要是参与多地区服务及关注多项基层民生议题工作；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，其开始代表民协积极参与香港立法会区议会选举，至<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，其成功当任深水埗区议会议员；任职期间，因其工作侧重于服务深水埗的居民，关注低收入等社会议题，经常要与政府沟通与合作，故其表示与政府关系良好；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，其又被当为民协副主席，至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年初，其在地区服务方面做出了许多与民生相关的活动与措施贡献；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年，其在民主派初选中参加了香港九龙西区议会的选举，因希望能有效实现民生理念而有意促成“五大要求”，故得票排名第四而得以出线代表民主派参选立法会，遂再度当选深水埗区议会议员，直到<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，其在香港民主派初选大搜捕中突遭香港警务处国家安全处拘捕，同年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，其等与组织及参与初选者共<span lang="EN-US">47</span>人被控违反港版国安法的“串谋颠覆国家政权罪”，但在被押<span lang="EN-US">2</span>周后，其暂获香港高等法院保释，而后被迫辞任了民协副主席一职；再后，其又度被收押候审；<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，香港高等法院<span lang="EN-US">3</span>名国安法指定法官裁定其等<span lang="EN-US">47</span>案被告「串谋颠覆国家政权」罪成；<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，其等「<span lang="EN-US">47</span>人初选案」被告在西九龙裁判法院被统一宣判；其因「不认罪」，并称民协是「温和民主派」<span lang="EN-US">,</span>民协「立会过半、光复香港」的口号是他由想出，而被最终判囚<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>个月（<span lang="EN-US">79</span>个月），刑期预至<span lang="EN-US">2030</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月；<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日获悉，其因不服判决，已提起上诉。目前被羁押地点缺详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2025/01/6747.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New
